## כאב (id: 003220000000000)

כאב
===

כאב (H3510)

verb · כְּאֵב · מַכְאֹוב

Impact

to be in pain \= state in which humans feel strong pain, usually as a result of a physical injury

[GEN 34:25](https://ref.ly/Gen34:25) · [JOB 14:22](https://ref.ly/Job14:22)

Impact

to hurt, to wound \= causative action by which humans or plants inflict wounds on humans and cause them to feel strong pain

[JOB 5:18](https://ref.ly/Job5:18) · [EZK 28:24](https://ref.ly/Ezek28:24)

Impact

to ruin \= causative action by which humans cause an object to no longer function as it should

[2KI 3:19](https://ref.ly/2Kgs3:19)

Grieve

to grieve \= state in which humans experience grief

[PSA 69:30](https://ref.ly/Ps69:30) · [PRO 14:13](https://ref.ly/Prov14:13)

Grieve

to cause grief \= causative action by which deities cause grief to humans

[EZK 13:22](https://ref.ly/Ezek13:22)

Enio R. Mueller

* **Associated Passages:** Genesis 34:25; Job 14:22; Job 5:18; Ezekiel 28:24; 2 Kings 3:19; Psalms 69:30; Proverbs 14:13; Ezekiel 13:22


## כְּאֵב (id: 003221000000000)

כְּאֵב
======

כְּאֵב (H3511)

noun m · כאב

Impact

wound \= state in which humans are physically wounded

[ISA 17:11](https://ref.ly/Isa17:11) · [JER 15:18](https://ref.ly/Jer15:18)

Grieve

grief \= state in which humans experience grief

[JOB 2:13](https://ref.ly/Job2:13) · [JOB 16:6](https://ref.ly/Job16:6) · [PSA 39:3](https://ref.ly/Ps39:3) · [ISA 65:14](https://ref.ly/Isa65:14)

Enio R. Mueller

* **Associated Passages:** Isaiah 17:11; Jeremiah 15:18; Job 2:13; Job 16:6; Psalms 39:3; Isaiah 65:14


## כאה (id: 003222000000000)

כאה
===

כאה (H3512a)

verb

Afraid

to be disheartened \= state in which humans lack confidence

[PSA 109:16](https://ref.ly/Ps109:16) · [DAN 11:30](https://ref.ly/Dan11:30)

Afraid

to dishearten \= causative action by which humans cause other humans to lack confidence

[EZK 13:22](https://ref.ly/Ezek13:22)

Enio R. Mueller

* **Associated Passages:** Psalms 109:16; Daniel 11:30; Ezekiel 13:22

## כבד (id: 003224000000000)

כבד
===

כבד (H3513)

verb · כָּבֵד · כֹּבֶד · כְּבֵדֻת · כָּבֹוד · כְּבוּדָּה · יֹוכֶבֶד

Heavy

to be heavy \= state in which objects have relatively much weight, ≈ which is often associated with slowness, functioning with difficulty, but also with importance, riches, status, etc.

[JOB 6:3](https://ref.ly/Job6:3) · [EZK 27:25](https://ref.ly/Ezek27:25)

Bear

to be burdensome literally: to be heavy; hence: \= state in which people are burdensome to other people

[2SA 13:25](https://ref.ly/2Sam13:25)

Chastise

**Collocation:** יָד כבד

to chastise literally: (someone's) hand is heavy (against someone else); hence: \= action by which a deity is chastising humans

[1SA 5:6](https://ref.ly/1Sam5:6) · [1SA 5:11](https://ref.ly/1Sam5:11) · [JOB 23:2](https://ref.ly/Job23:2)1 · [PSA 32:4](https://ref.ly/Ps32:4)

Control

to lay heavy burdens literally: to make heavy; hence: \= action by which humans exercise authority on others with a heavy hand

[NEH 5:15](https://ref.ly/Neh5:15)

Respect

to honor, to respect \= action by which humans, deities, or animals treat other humans, deities, times, or objects with honor and respect

[EXO 20:12](https://ref.ly/Exod20:12) · [NUM 22:17](https://ref.ly/Num22:17) · [NUM 22:17](https://ref.ly/Num22:17) · [NUM 22:37](https://ref.ly/Num22:37) · [NUM 24:11](https://ref.ly/Num24:11) · [NUM 24:11](https://ref.ly/Num24:11) · [DEU 5:16](https://ref.ly/Deut5:16) · [JDG 9:9](https://ref.ly/Judg9:9) · [JDG 13:17](https://ref.ly/Judg13:17) · [1SA 2:29](https://ref.ly/1Sam2:29) · [1SA 2:30](https://ref.ly/1Sam2:30) · [1SA 2:30](https://ref.ly/1Sam2:30) · [1SA 15:30](https://ref.ly/1Sam15:30) · [2SA 10:3](https://ref.ly/2Sam10:3) · [1CH 19:3](https://ref.ly/1Chr19:3) · [PSA 15:4](https://ref.ly/Ps15:4) · [PSA 22:24](https://ref.ly/Ps22:24) · [PSA 50:15](https://ref.ly/Ps50:15) · [PSA 50:23](https://ref.ly/Ps50:23) · [PSA 86:9](https://ref.ly/Ps86:9) · [PSA 86:12](https://ref.ly/Ps86:12) · [PSA 91:15](https://ref.ly/Ps91:15) · [PRO 3:9](https://ref.ly/Prov3:9) · [PRO 4:8](https://ref.ly/Prov4:8) · [PRO 13:18](https://ref.ly/Prov13:18) · [PRO 14:31](https://ref.ly/Prov14:31) · [PRO 27:18](https://ref.ly/Prov27:18) · [ISA 24:15](https://ref.ly/Isa24:15) · [ISA 25:3](https://ref.ly/Isa25:3) · [ISA 29:13](https://ref.ly/Isa29:13) · [ISA 43:20](https://ref.ly/Isa43:20) · [ISA 43:23](https://ref.ly/Isa43:23) · [ISA 58:13](https://ref.ly/Isa58:13) · [ISA 58:13](https://ref.ly/Isa58:13) · [ISA 60:13](https://ref.ly/Isa60:13) · [LAM 1:8](https://ref.ly/Lam1:8) · [DAN 11:38](https://ref.ly/Dan11:38) · [DAN 11:38](https://ref.ly/Dan11:38) · [MAL 1:6](https://ref.ly/Mal1:6)

Control

**Collocation:** כבד עֹל

to make (someone's) yoke heavy, to oppress literally: to make (someone's) yoke heavy; hence: \= action by which human rules exercise authority on other with a heavy hand

[1KI 12:10](https://ref.ly/1Kgs12:10) · [1KI 12:14](https://ref.ly/1Kgs12:14) · [2CH 10:10](https://ref.ly/2Chr10:10) · [2CH 10:14](https://ref.ly/2Chr10:14) · [ISA 47:6](https://ref.ly/Isa47:6)

Extraordinary

glorious \= state in which words are of a high quality, and ► spoken in order to inspire an attitude of respect towards something

[PSA 87:3](https://ref.ly/Ps87:3)

Great

to be honorable, to be worthy of honor, to be renowned \= state in which humans and deities are regarded as worthy of honor and respect

[GEN 34:19](https://ref.ly/Gen34:19) · [EXO 14:4](https://ref.ly/Exod14:4) · [EXO 14:17](https://ref.ly/Exod14:17) · [EXO 14:18](https://ref.ly/Exod14:18) · [LEV 10:3](https://ref.ly/Lev10:3) · [NUM 22:15](https://ref.ly/Num22:15) · [DEU 28:58](https://ref.ly/Deut28:58) · [1SA 9:6](https://ref.ly/1Sam9:6) · [1SA 22:14](https://ref.ly/1Sam22:14) · [2SA 6:22](https://ref.ly/2Sam6:22) · [2SA 23:19](https://ref.ly/2Sam23:19) · [2SA 23:23](https://ref.ly/2Sam23:23) · [2KI 14:10](https://ref.ly/2Kgs14:10) · [1CH 4:9](https://ref.ly/1Chr4:9) · [1CH 11:21](https://ref.ly/1Chr11:21) · [1CH 11:25](https://ref.ly/1Chr11:25) · [JOB 14:21](https://ref.ly/Job14:21) · [PSA 149:8](https://ref.ly/Ps149:8) · [ISA 3:5](https://ref.ly/Isa3:5) · [ISA 23:8](https://ref.ly/Isa23:8) · [ISA 23:9](https://ref.ly/Isa23:9) · [ISA 26:15](https://ref.ly/Isa26:15) · [ISA 43:4](https://ref.ly/Isa43:4) · [ISA 49:5](https://ref.ly/Isa49:5) · [ISA 66:5](https://ref.ly/Isa66:5) · [EZK 28:22](https://ref.ly/Ezek28:22) · [NAM 3:10](https://ref.ly/Nah3:10) · [HAG 1:8](https://ref.ly/Hag1:8)

Great

to put on airs, to play the important man \= pattern of actions in which humans behave as people worthy of honor

[PRO 12:9](https://ref.ly/Prov12:9)

Great

to gain honor, to gain glory \= action by which humans and deities bring honor and respect upon themselves

[2SA 6:20](https://ref.ly/2Sam6:20) · [2CH 25:19](https://ref.ly/2Chr25:19) · [EZK 39:13](https://ref.ly/Ezek39:13)

Great

to make glorious \= causative action by which deities bring honor to people and areas

[ISA 8:23](https://ref.ly/Isa8:23) · [JER 30:19](https://ref.ly/Jer30:19)

Intense

to be heavy, to be serious, to be grievous, to be burdensome, to be strong \= state in which an event is weighing heavily on the mind of those undergoing it

[GEN 18:20](https://ref.ly/Gen18:20) · [EXO 5:9](https://ref.ly/Exod5:9) · [JDG 20:34](https://ref.ly/Judg20:34) · [1SA 31:3](https://ref.ly/1Sam31:3) · [1CH 10:3](https://ref.ly/1Chr10:3) · [NEH 5:18](https://ref.ly/Neh5:18) · [JOB 33:7](https://ref.ly/Job33:7) · [PSA 38:5](https://ref.ly/Ps38:5) · [ISA 24:20](https://ref.ly/Isa24:20)

Quantity

to abound \= state in which an object contains a large quantity of a substance

[PRO 8:24](https://ref.ly/Prov8:24)

Quantity

to multiply oneself, to make oneself numerous \= action by which humans make themselves numerous

[NAM 3:15](https://ref.ly/Nah3:15) · [NAM 3:15](https://ref.ly/Nah3:15)

Quantity

to amass, to heap up \= causative action by which humans cause objects to increase in number

[HAB 2:6](https://ref.ly/Hab2:6)

Strong

**Collocation:** יָד כבד

to increase in power literally: (someone's) hand is heavy; hence: \= state in which a nation's power increases to the extent that it enables them to exercise authority over others

[JDG 1:35](https://ref.ly/Judg1:35)

Unable

to be dim, to be dull literally: to be heavy; hence: \= state in which part of the body does not function well

[GEN 48:10](https://ref.ly/Gen48:10) · [ISA 59:1](https://ref.ly/Isa59:1)

Unable

to make dull literally: to make heavy; hence: \= causative action by which humans cause part of their body not to function well

[ISA 6:10](https://ref.ly/Isa6:10) · [ZEC 7:11](https://ref.ly/Zech7:11)

Unsafe

**Collocation:** כבד נְחֹשֶׁת

to weigh down with chains \> to bring heavy suffering literally: to make (someone's) bronze heavy; hence: \= causative action by which deities brings intense suffering on humans, ◄ compared to a prisoner wearing heavy chains

[LAM 3:7](https://ref.ly/Lam3:7)

Unwilling

**Collocation:** לֵב כבד

to be stubborn literally: (one's) heart is heavy; hence: \= state in which humans are stubborn and unwilling to listen

[EXO 9:7](https://ref.ly/Exod9:7)

Unwilling

**Collocation:** כבד לֵב · כבד לֵבָב

to behave stubbornly literally: to make (one's) heart heavy; hence: \= action by which humans act in a stubborn way and are unwilling to listen

[EXO 8:11](https://ref.ly/Exod8:11) · [EXO 8:28](https://ref.ly/Exod8:28) · [EXO 9:34](https://ref.ly/Exod9:34) · [1SA 6:6](https://ref.ly/1Sam6:6) · [1SA 6:6](https://ref.ly/1Sam6:6)

Unwilling

**Collocation:** כבד לֵב

to make stubborn literally: to make (someone else's) heart heavy; hence: \= causative action by which deities cause humans to act in a stubborn way and make them unwilling to listen

[EXO 10:1](https://ref.ly/Exod10:1)

1 JOB 23:2 This interpretation requires that יָדִי is read as יָדוֹ. 2 HAG 1:8 MT\-K אכבד \| MT\-Q אַכָּבְדָה

Reinier de Blois

* **Associated Passages:** Job 6:3; Ezekiel 27:25; 2 Samuel 13:25; 1 Samuel 5:6; 1 Samuel 5:11; Job 23:2; Psalms 32:4; Nehemiah 5:15; Exodus 20:12; Numbers 22:17; Numbers 22:37; Numbers 24:11; Deuteronomy 5:16; Judges 9:9; Judges 13:17; 1 Samuel 2:29; 1 Samuel 2:30; 1 Samuel 15:30; 2 Samuel 10:3; 1 Chronicles 19:3; Psalms 15:4; Psalms 22:24; Psalms 50:15; Psalms 50:23; Psalms 86:9; Psalms 86:12; Psalms 91:15; Proverbs 3:9; Proverbs 4:8; Proverbs 13:18; Proverbs 14:31; Proverbs 27:18; Isaiah 24:15; Isaiah 25:3; Isaiah 29:13; Isaiah 43:20; Isaiah 43:23; Isaiah 58:13; Isaiah 60:13; Lamentations 1:8; Daniel 11:38; Malachi 1:6; 1 Kings 12:10; 1 Kings 12:14; 2 Chronicles 10:10; 2 Chronicles 10:14; Isaiah 47:6; Psalms 87:3; Genesis 34:19; Exodus 14:4; Exodus 14:17; Exodus 14:18; Leviticus 10:3; Numbers 22:15; Deuteronomy 28:58; 1 Samuel 9:6; 1 Samuel 22:14; 2 Samuel 6:22; 2 Samuel 23:19; 2 Samuel 23:23; 2 Kings 14:10; 1 Chronicles 4:9; 1 Chronicles 11:21; 1 Chronicles 11:25; Job 14:21; Psalms 149:8; Isaiah 3:5; Isaiah 23:8; Isaiah 23:9; Isaiah 26:15; Isaiah 43:4; Isaiah 49:5; Isaiah 66:5; Ezekiel 28:22; Nahum 3:10; Haggai 1:8; Proverbs 12:9; 2 Samuel 6:20; 2 Chronicles 25:19; Ezekiel 39:13; Isaiah 8:23; Jeremiah 30:19; Genesis 18:20; Exodus 5:9; Judges 20:34; 1 Samuel 31:3; 1 Chronicles 10:3; Nehemiah 5:18; Job 33:7; Psalms 38:5; Isaiah 24:20; Proverbs 8:24; Nahum 3:15; Habakkuk 2:6; Judges 1:35; Genesis 48:10; Isaiah 59:1; Isaiah 6:10; Zechariah 7:11; Lamentations 3:7; Exodus 9:7; Exodus 8:11; Exodus 8:28; Exodus 9:34; 1 Samuel 6:6; Exodus 10:1


## כָּבֵד (id: 003225000000000)

כָּבֵד
======

כָּבֵד (H3515 · H3516)

adj · כבד

Heavy

heavy \= state in which an object has relatively much weight, ≈ which is often associated with slowness, functioning with difficulty, but also with importance, riches, status, etc.

[1SA 4:18](https://ref.ly/1Sam4:18) · [2SA 14:26](https://ref.ly/2Sam14:26) · [1KI 12:4](https://ref.ly/1Kgs12:4) · [1KI 12:11](https://ref.ly/1Kgs12:11) · [2CH 10:4](https://ref.ly/2Chr10:4) · [2CH 10:11](https://ref.ly/2Chr10:11) · [PSA 38:5](https://ref.ly/Ps38:5)

Complicated

**Collocation:** כִּבְדֵי לָשֹׁון

"heavy of tongue" \> difficult language literally: heavy of tongue; hence: \= state in which people speak a language that others find hard to understand

[EZK 3:5](https://ref.ly/Ezek3:5) · [EZK 3:6](https://ref.ly/Ezek3:6)

Large

large \= state in which an object is large in size

[EXO 19:16](https://ref.ly/Exod19:16) · [ISA 32:2](https://ref.ly/Isa32:2)

Intense

to be heavy, to be serious, to be grievous, to be burdensome, to be strong \= state in which an event is weighing heavily on the mind of those undergoing it

[GEN 12:10](https://ref.ly/Gen12:10) · [GEN 41:31](https://ref.ly/Gen41:31) · [GEN 43:1](https://ref.ly/Gen43:1) · [GEN 47:4](https://ref.ly/Gen47:4) · [GEN 47:13](https://ref.ly/Gen47:13) · [GEN 50:10](https://ref.ly/Gen50:10) · [GEN 50:11](https://ref.ly/Gen50:11) · [EXO 9:3](https://ref.ly/Exod9:3) · [EXO 9:18](https://ref.ly/Exod9:18) · [EXO 9:24](https://ref.ly/Exod9:24) · [EXO 18:18](https://ref.ly/Exod18:18) · [NUM 11:14](https://ref.ly/Num11:14) · [PRO 27:3](https://ref.ly/Prov27:3) · [ISA 1:4](https://ref.ly/Isa1:4)

Quantity

large, great, numerous \= state in which a group of humans, animals, or objects is large in size

[GEN 50:9](https://ref.ly/Gen50:9) · [EXO 8:20](https://ref.ly/Exod8:20) · [EXO 10:14](https://ref.ly/Exod10:14) · [EXO 12:38](https://ref.ly/Exod12:38) · [NUM 20:20](https://ref.ly/Num20:20) · [1KI 3:9](https://ref.ly/1Kgs3:9) · [1KI 10:2](https://ref.ly/1Kgs10:2) · [2KI 6:14](https://ref.ly/2Kgs6:14) · [2KI 18:17](https://ref.ly/2Kgs18:17) · [2CH 9:1](https://ref.ly/2Chr9:1) · [ISA 36:2](https://ref.ly/Isa36:2)

Rich

to be rich \= state in which humans have many assets, ≈ associated with honor and respect

[GEN 13:2](https://ref.ly/Gen13:2)

Strong

**Collocation:** יָדַיִם כְּבֵדִים

"hands are heavy" \> hands are weary literally: (one's) hands are heavy; hence: \= state in which one's hands become tired as a result of a certain activity ◄ which makes them seem heavy

[EXO 17:12](https://ref.ly/Exod17:12)

Unable

slow literally: to be heavy; hence: \= state in which part of the body, such as one's mouth or one's tongue, does not function well

[EXO 4:10](https://ref.ly/Exod4:10) · [EXO 4:10](https://ref.ly/Exod4:10)

Unwilling

**Collocation:** לֵב כָּבֵד

to be stubborn literally: (one's) heart is heavy; hence: \= state in which humans are stubborn and unwilling to listen

[EXO 7:14](https://ref.ly/Exod7:14)

noun f · כבד

liver \= a large lobed glandular organ in the abdomen, involved in processing digestive products, neutralizing toxins, and other metabolic processes

[EXO 29:13](https://ref.ly/Exod29:13) · [EXO 29:22](https://ref.ly/Exod29:22) · [LEV 3:4](https://ref.ly/Lev3:4) · [LEV 3:10](https://ref.ly/Lev3:10) · [LEV 3:15](https://ref.ly/Lev3:15) · [LEV 4:9](https://ref.ly/Lev4:9) · [LEV 7:4](https://ref.ly/Lev7:4) · [LEV 8:16](https://ref.ly/Lev8:16) · [LEV 8:25](https://ref.ly/Lev8:25) · [LEV 9:10](https://ref.ly/Lev9:10) · [LEV 9:19](https://ref.ly/Lev9:19) · [PRO 7:23](https://ref.ly/Prov7:23) · [LAM 2:11](https://ref.ly/Lam2:11) · [EZK 21:26](https://ref.ly/Ezek21:26)

Reinier de Blois

* **Associated Passages:** 1 Samuel 4:18; 2 Samuel 14:26; 1 Kings 12:4; 1 Kings 12:11; 2 Chronicles 10:4; 2 Chronicles 10:11; Psalms 38:5; Ezekiel 3:5; Ezekiel 3:6; Exodus 19:16; Isaiah 32:2; Genesis 12:10; Genesis 41:31; Genesis 43:1; Genesis 47:4; Genesis 47:13; Genesis 50:10; Genesis 50:11; Exodus 9:3; Exodus 9:18; Exodus 9:24; Exodus 18:18; Numbers 11:14; Proverbs 27:3; Isaiah 1:4; Genesis 50:9; Exodus 8:20; Exodus 10:14; Exodus 12:38; Numbers 20:20; 1 Kings 3:9; 1 Kings 10:2; 2 Kings 6:14; 2 Kings 18:17; 2 Chronicles 9:1; Isaiah 36:2; Genesis 13:2; Exodus 17:12; Exodus 4:10; Exodus 7:14; Exodus 29:13; Exodus 29:22; Leviticus 3:4; Leviticus 3:10; Leviticus 3:15; Leviticus 4:9; Leviticus 7:4; Leviticus 8:16; Leviticus 8:25; Leviticus 9:10; Leviticus 9:19; Proverbs 7:23; Lamentations 2:11; Ezekiel 21:26

## כבה (id: 003228000000000)

כבה
===

כבה (H3518)

verb

Quench

to be extinguished \= process by which a fire comes to an end, either in a natural way or by force

[LEV 6:5](https://ref.ly/Lev6:5) · [LEV 6:6](https://ref.ly/Lev6:6) · [1SA 3:3](https://ref.ly/1Sam3:3) · [2KI 22:17](https://ref.ly/2Kgs22:17) · [2CH 34:25](https://ref.ly/2Chr34:25) · [PRO 26:20](https://ref.ly/Prov26:20) · [PRO 31:18](https://ref.ly/Prov31:18) · [ISA 34:10](https://ref.ly/Isa34:10) · [ISA 43:17](https://ref.ly/Isa43:17) · [ISA 66:24](https://ref.ly/Isa66:24) · [JER 7:20](https://ref.ly/Jer7:20) · [JER 17:27](https://ref.ly/Jer17:27) · [EZK 21:3](https://ref.ly/Ezek21:3) · [EZK 21:4](https://ref.ly/Ezek21:4)

Quench

to extinguish \= causative process by which humans or deities cause a fire to come to an end, either in a natural way or by force

[2SA 14:7](https://ref.ly/2Sam14:7) · [2SA 21:17](https://ref.ly/2Sam21:17) · [2CH 29:7](https://ref.ly/2Chr29:7) · [SNG 8:7](https://ref.ly/Song8:7) · [ISA 1:31](https://ref.ly/Isa1:31) · [ISA 42:3](https://ref.ly/Isa42:3) · [JER 4:4](https://ref.ly/Jer4:4) · [JER 21:12](https://ref.ly/Jer21:12) · [EZK 32:7](https://ref.ly/Ezek32:7) · [AMO 5:6](https://ref.ly/Amos5:6)

Enio R. Mueller

## כָּבֹוד (id: 003229000000000)

כָּבֹוד
=======

כָּבֹוד (H3519)

noun c · כבד

Great

honor, power, dignity \= position of honor; ◄ often as a result of wealth and/or authority

Role

to act as priest, to serve as priest \= state in which humans have been ordained and consecrated to function as a priest

[EXO 28:1](https://ref.ly/Exod28:1) · [EXO 28:3](https://ref.ly/Exod28:3) · [EXO 28:4](https://ref.ly/Exod28:4) · [EXO 28:41](https://ref.ly/Exod28:41) · [EXO 29:1](https://ref.ly/Exod29:1) · [EXO 29:44](https://ref.ly/Exod29:44) · [EXO 30:30](https://ref.ly/Exod30:30) · [EXO 31:10](https://ref.ly/Exod31:10) · [EXO 35:19](https://ref.ly/Exod35:19) · [EXO 39:41](https://ref.ly/Exod39:41) · [EXO 40:13](https://ref.ly/Exod40:13) · [EXO 40:15](https://ref.ly/Exod40:15) · [LEV 7:35](https://ref.ly/Lev7:35) · [LEV 16:32](https://ref.ly/Lev16:32) · [NUM 3:3](https://ref.ly/Num3:3) · [NUM 3:4](https://ref.ly/Num3:4) · [DEU 10:6](https://ref.ly/Deut10:6) · [1CH 5:36](https://ref.ly/1Chr5:36) · [1CH 24:2](https://ref.ly/1Chr24:2) · [2CH 11:14](https://ref.ly/2Chr11:14) · [EZK 44:13](https://ref.ly/Ezek44:13) · [HOS 4:6](https://ref.ly/Hos4:6)

Priests

to act like a priest meaning unsure; possibly: \= action by which humans mimick a priest by dressing up in a certain way

[ISA 61:10](https://ref.ly/Isa61:10)1

1 ISA 61:10 NIV ESV \| BHS יכין RSV NRSV "decks himself" NJPS "adorned" GNT "dressed" \| REB omit

Enio R. Mueller

* **Associated Passages:** Exodus 28:1; Exodus 28:3; Exodus 28:4; Exodus 28:41; Exodus 29:1; Exodus 29:44; Exodus 30:30; Exodus 31:10; Exodus 35:19; Exodus 39:41; Exodus 40:13; Exodus 40:15; Leviticus 7:35; Leviticus 16:32; Numbers 3:3; Numbers 3:4; Deuteronomy 10:6; 1 Chronicles 5:36; 1 Chronicles 24:2; 2 Chronicles 11:14; Ezekiel 44:13; Hosea 4:6; Isaiah 61:10


## כָּהֵן (id: 003256000000000)

כָּהֵן
======

כָּהֵן (A3549)

noun m

Priests

priest \= person ordained and consecrated to perform religious services on behalf of others

[EZR 6:9](https://ref.ly/Ezra6:9) · [EZR 6:16](https://ref.ly/Ezra6:16) · [EZR 6:18](https://ref.ly/Ezra6:18) · [EZR 7:12](https://ref.ly/Ezra7:12) · [EZR 7:13](https://ref.ly/Ezra7:13) · [EZR 7:16](https://ref.ly/Ezra7:16) · [EZR 7:21](https://ref.ly/Ezra7:21) · [EZR 7:24](https://ref.ly/Ezra7:24)

verb

## כּוּר (id: 003271000000000)

כּוּר
=====

כּוּר (H3564)

noun m · כִּיר

Furnaces

smelting furnace, kiln \= a construction ◄ made of hardened clay or of bricks ► and used for the smelting of ore or the firing of ceramic ware; ≈ often used figuratively to denote a prolonged period of hardship; also associated with times of testing and trial

## כֶּלֶב (id: 003312000000000)

כֶּלֶב
======

כֶּלֶב (H3611)

noun m

Domestic Animals

dog \= relatively small light brown domestic animal, feeding on anything from household refuse to animal carcasses and excreta; ◄ \|iCanis familiaris putiatini\|i\*; ► extremely unclean animal and therefore not to be eaten, though used for hunting and for watching sheep; ≈ considered almost as unclean as a pig; associated with all sorts of uncleanness, aggression, greediness, low status; used as derogatory term for male shrine prostitutes

## כְּלִיא (id: 003327000000000)

כְּלִיא
=======

כְּלִיא (H3628)

noun m · כלא

Prisons

**Collocation:** בֵּית הַכְּלִיא

prison \= place where criminals or other prisoners were confined

1 JER 37:4 · JER 52:31 MT\-K הכליא \= כְּלִיא \| MT\-Q הַכְּלוּא \= כְּלוּא

Reinier de Blois



## כִּלְיָה (id: 003328000000000)

כִּלְיָה
========

כִּלְיָה (H3629)

noun f

kidney \= either of a pair of relatively small organs in the abdominal cavity of humans and animals and usually burned along with the fat of an animal sacrifice on the altar; ≈ regarded as a delicacy and considered the seat of emotions and one's devotion to God

## כנה (id: 003349000000000)

כנה
===

כנה (H3655)

verb

Name

to take a name \= action by which humans adopt a name or title for themselves

[ISA 44:5](https://ref.ly/Isa44:5)

Name

to give a title \= cauative action by which humans or deities assign a name or title to (other) humans, either to honor or flatter them

[JOB 32:21](https://ref.ly/Job32:21) · [JOB 32:22](https://ref.ly/Job32:22) · [ISA 45:4](https://ref.ly/Isa45:4)

Enio R. Mueller

* **Associated Passages:** Isaiah 44:5; Job 32:21; Job 32:22; Isaiah 45:4

## כִּנֹּור (id: 003352000000000)

כִּנֹּור
========

כִּנֹּור (H3658)

noun m

Musical Instruments

small lyre, lute \= musical instrument consisting of a sound box ◄ made of wood, out of the ends or sides of which projected two arms; the arms supported a crosspiece; strings descended from the crosspiece over the sound box and the number of strings could vary; ► often used to accompany singing

## כֶּסֶא (id: 003369000000000)

כֶּסֶא
======

כֶּסֶא (H3677)

noun m

Time

full moon \= the day when the moon was in full shine; ≈ marked with religious celebrations

[PSA 81:4](https://ref.ly/Ps81:4) · [PRO 7:20](https://ref.ly/Prov7:20)

Enio R. Mueller

* **Associated Passages:** Psalms 81:4; Proverbs 7:20


## כסה (id: 003370000000000)

כסה
===

כסה (H3680)

verb · כָּסוּי · כְּסוּת · מִכְסֶה · מְכַסֶּה

Cover

to cover, to be covered \= state or process by which a surface is covered by another object, ► often making this surface more or less invisible

Cover

to cover oneself \= action by which humans cover part of their body with a veil, ► in order to make it invisible

Cover

to cover \= causative action by which humans or deities cover a surface with their hands, a piece of cloth, a substance, or an object, ► often with the purpose of making this surface invisible or inaccessible

## כְּסוּת (id: 003372000000000)

כְּסוּת
=======

כְּסוּת (H3682)

noun f · כסה

Innocent

proof of innocence, vindication literally: covering; hence: \= something that is a visible proof of someone else's innocence in a certain matter

[GEN 20:16](https://ref.ly/Gen20:16)

Dress

clothing literally: covering; hence: the clothing that are needed for protection against the cold and enable people to function within their community

[EXO 21:10](https://ref.ly/Exod21:10) · [EXO 22:26](https://ref.ly/Exod22:26) · [DEU 22:12](https://ref.ly/Deut22:12) · [JOB 24:7](https://ref.ly/Job24:7) · [JOB 31:19](https://ref.ly/Job31:19) · [ISA 50:3](https://ref.ly/Isa50:3)

Non\-Know

covering literally: covering; hence: \= state in which no information is shared about an object, ◄ as if it is covered and invisible to outsiders

[JOB 26:6](https://ref.ly/Job26:6)

Reinier de Blois

* **Associated Passages:** Genesis 20:16; Exodus 21:10; Exodus 22:26; Deuteronomy 22:12; Job 24:7; Job 31:19; Isaiah 50:3; Job 26:6

adj · כסל

Foolish

foolish, dull \= state of absence of wisdom, which manifests itself in excessive anger, talking too rashly and too much, sinful behavior, and laziness, ► and results in poverty, shame, punishment, and trouble and grief for other people; ≈ foolishness is thought to reside in a person's heart; the behavior and treatment of fools is often compared to that of animals

## כעס (id: 003395000000000)

כעס
===

כעס (H3707)

verb · כַּעַס

Angry

to be, become vexed, to be, become angry \= state/process by which humans or deities experience displeasure; ◄ caused by someone else's condition or behavior

[2CH 16:10](https://ref.ly/2Chr16:10) · [NEH 3:33](https://ref.ly/Neh3:33) · [PSA 112:10](https://ref.ly/Ps112:10) · [ECC 5:16](https://ref.ly/Eccl5:16) · [ECC 7:9](https://ref.ly/Eccl7:9) · [EZK 16:42](https://ref.ly/Ezek16:42)

Angry

**Collocation:** כעס

to trouble, to vex, to provoke to anger \= causative action by which humans or deities cause other humans or deities to experience displeasure ◄ by their words or behavior

כִּפֻּרִים
==========

כִּפֻּרִים (H3725)

noun m · כפר

Innocent

atonement \= causative action by which a priest performs the rituals that are required to remove guilt or uncleanness from people or objects, which usually requires a blood sacrifice or another kind of compensation

[EXO 29:36](https://ref.ly/Exod29:36) · [EXO 30:10](https://ref.ly/Exod30:10) · [EXO 30:16](https://ref.ly/Exod30:16) · [LEV 23:27](https://ref.ly/Lev23:27) · [LEV 23:28](https://ref.ly/Lev23:28) · [LEV 25:9](https://ref.ly/Lev25:9) · [NUM 5:8](https://ref.ly/Num5:8) · [NUM 29:11](https://ref.ly/Num29:11)

Reinier de Blois

* **Associated Passages:** Exodus 29:36; Exodus 30:10; Exodus 30:16; Leviticus 23:27; Leviticus 23:28; Leviticus 25:9; Numbers 5:8; Numbers 29:11


## כַּפֹּרֶת (id: 003417000000000)

כַּפֹּרֶת
=========

כַּפֹּרֶת (H3727)

noun f · כפר

Cover

cover, lid (of the ark of the covenant) \= a flat, rectangular object with two golden figures with wings on its top, made out of hammered gold, ► and used to cover the Covenant Box, which represented the presence of YHWH among his people; this is also the place where, once a year, on the Day of Atonement, blood from sacrificial animals was sprinkled; ≈ associated with atonement

[EXO 25:17](https://ref.ly/Exod25:17) · [EXO 25:18](https://ref.ly/Exod25:18) · [EXO 25:19](https://ref.ly/Exod25:19) · [EXO 25:20](https://ref.ly/Exod25:20) · [EXO 25:20](https://ref.ly/Exod25:20) · [EXO 25:21](https://ref.ly/Exod25:21) · [EXO 25:22](https://ref.ly/Exod25:22) · [EXO 26:34](https://ref.ly/Exod26:34) · [EXO 30:6](https://ref.ly/Exod30:6) · [EXO 31:7](https://ref.ly/Exod31:7) · [EXO 35:12](https://ref.ly/Exod35:12) · [EXO 37:6](https://ref.ly/Exod37:6) · [EXO 37:7](https://ref.ly/Exod37:7) · [EXO 37:8](https://ref.ly/Exod37:8) · [EXO 37:9](https://ref.ly/Exod37:9) · [EXO 37:9](https://ref.ly/Exod37:9) · [EXO 39:35](https://ref.ly/Exod39:35) · [EXO 40:20](https://ref.ly/Exod40:20) · [LEV 16:2](https://ref.ly/Lev16:2) · [LEV 16:2](https://ref.ly/Lev16:2) · [LEV 16:13](https://ref.ly/Lev16:13) · [LEV 16:14](https://ref.ly/Lev16:14) · [LEV 16:14](https://ref.ly/Lev16:14) · [LEV 16:15](https://ref.ly/Lev16:15) · [LEV 16:15](https://ref.ly/Lev16:15) · [NUM 7:89](https://ref.ly/Num7:89) · [1CH 28:11](https://ref.ly/1Chr28:11)

## כרה (id: 003426000000000)

כרה
===

כרה (A3735 · H3738a · H3738b · H3739a · H3739b) — כרא

verb · כָּרָה · מִכְרֶה

Exist

to dig, to hew out \= action by which humans break up and move earth or stone, usually with a tool, and with the purpose of creating a hole

[GEN 26:25](https://ref.ly/Gen26:25) · [GEN 50:5](https://ref.ly/Gen50:5) · [EXO 21:33](https://ref.ly/Exod21:33) · [NUM 21:18](https://ref.ly/Num21:18) · [2CH 16:14](https://ref.ly/2Chr16:14) · [PSA 7:16](https://ref.ly/Ps7:16) · [PSA 57:7](https://ref.ly/Ps57:7) · [PSA 94:13](https://ref.ly/Ps94:13) · [PSA 119:85](https://ref.ly/Ps119:85) · [PRO 26:27](https://ref.ly/Prov26:27) · [JER 18:20](https://ref.ly/Jer18:20) · [JER 18:22](https://ref.ly/Jer18:22)

Think

**Collocation:** כרה רָעָה

to plot, to concoct, to rake up literally: to dig out evil; hence: \= action by which humans are exercising their minds in order to determine what must be done to do evil

[PRO 16:27](https://ref.ly/Prov16:27)

Willing

**Collocation:** כרה אָזְנַיִם

to give an open ear literally: to hew out two ears; hence, probably: \= causative action by which deities cause humans to be willing and obedient by giving them ears that are willing to listen

[PSA 40:7](https://ref.ly/Ps40:7)1

verb

Possess

to purchase, to buy \= action by which humans acquire an animate or inanimate object ◄ by means of a financial transaction or in another way

[DEU 2:6](https://ref.ly/Deut2:6) · [HOS 3:2](https://ref.ly/Hos3:2)

Speak

to barter, to bargain \= action by which a potential buyer and seller negotiate about the price

[JOB 6:27](https://ref.ly/Job6:27) · [JOB 40:30](https://ref.ly/Job40:30)

verb · כֵּרָה

Festivals

**Collocation:** כרה כֵּרָה

to hold a feast \= causative action by which humans hold a celebration involving eating and drinking

[2KI 6:23](https://ref.ly/2Kgs6:23)

verb

Afraid

**Collocation:** רוּחַ כרה

(one's) spirit is troubled, (one's) spirit is anxious \= process by which the human mind is deeply troubled by a certain event

[DAN 7:15](https://ref.ly/Dan7:15)

1 PSA 40:7 RSV NRSV ESV "you have given me an open ear" NJPS "you gave me to understand" REB "you have given me receptive ears" GNT "you have given me ears to hear you" CEV "you made me willing to listen and obey" \| NIV "my ears you have pierced" (cf. [EXO 21:6](https://ref.ly/Exod21:6))

Reinier de Blois

* **Associated Passages:** Genesis 26:25; Genesis 50:5; Exodus 21:33; Numbers 21:18; 2 Chronicles 16:14; Psalms 7:16; Psalms 57:7; Psalms 94:13; Psalms 119:85; Proverbs 26:27; Jeremiah 18:20; Jeremiah 18:22; Proverbs 16:27; Psalms 40:7; Deuteronomy 2:6; Hosea 3:2; Job 6:27; Job 40:30; 2 Kings 6:23; Daniel 7:15

## כְּרוּב (id: 003428000000000)

כְּרוּב
=======

כְּרוּב (H3742 · H3743) [SAHD](https://sahd-online.com/words/krub/)

noun m

cherub, winged creature \= heavenly creature with wings, ► carrying the throne of God, symbol of God's majesty, and associated with his presence The cherubim have a close connection to the temple and the manifestation of the deity due to their apotropaic function. Their association with vegetation in the temple iconography and in Gn 3\.24 is linked to the idea that they served as boundary markers, designating and guarding sacred space.

noun f

## כַּרְפַּס (id: 003450000000000)

כַּרְפַּס
=========

כַּרְפַּס (H3768)

noun m

Plants

cotton \= an annual plant, which grows to 2 meters in height, with soft, lobed leaves and mallow\-like flowers, which are yellow with a purple center; when the flower matures, the boll underneath puffs out and eventually splits, revealing a mass of fine white filaments that we know as “cotton wool;” ◄ Gossypium herbaceum; ► used for making cloth

[EST 1:6](https://ref.ly/Esth1:6)

Reinier de Blois

* **Associated Passages:** Esther 1:6

כְּתֹבֶת
========

כְּתֹבֶת (H3793)

noun f · כתב
